			else = {

						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
						province = {
							all_provinces = yes
							first = yes #just picks the first valid after reduction
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			add_to_variable = { 
				CHI_ROCAF_sp_tag_rocket_speed_factor = 0.10
				tooltip = sp_tag_rocket_speed_factor_tt
			}
		}
	}
